name:H‚Äço‚Äçw‚Äça‚Äçr‚Äçd
info:Cliffside Suite
info:Stayed in June 2023
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted June 11, 2023
msg:Fantastic 2-night stay at the Naked Castle.  Perfect for a short getaway from surrounding big cities.  Beautiful views from the cliffside suite. I prefer the cliffside suite vs. the 5 different themed castle room due to the large open layout of the suite and better views of the mountain. Staffs are super nice and friendly.  Buffet breakfast (next to the pool) is good and the restaurant at the castle is great! Not a huge amount of amenities but that's ok since the purpose of going there is to relax.  Used half a day to check out the nearby Mo Gan Shan scenic areas. If you don't drive yourself, getting in and out with taxi requires a little bit of planning.  Side of the property has two direct hiking trails to the nearby Mo Gan Shan scenic area (easy hike) and Yu Cun (very challenging).  Pro tip: make sure to bring anti-mosquito/bugs bite lotion/cream and also anti-itch lotion.

Special shout-out to Johnson, who really took care of us during our stay and the restaurant staff at the castle for their excellent service!

The hotel has activities every hour, and I participated in some of them. It was pretty good. I was the only one visiting the castle. The next day, I took the hotel bus to Naked Stables and took a look around. I felt that the cliff view room at Naked Stables was the best.
The hotel has a fixed commuter bus every day, but not many. Naked Stables has a test ride Land Rover at 9 o'clock in the morning. It's a pity that I can't go there without commuting at this time. Another thing is that I don't know why there is a piece of glass on the door of the hotel room, which is light-transmissive. So I woke up early in the morning and woke up at dawn.
The breakfast was also good.
The most unexpected thing was that I saw two eagles on the balcony in the morning, very close, and Xiao Chen said that I would have good luck.
Overall, it was a great experience.

About meals:
The hotel is an independent resort. Although there will be farmhouses 15 minutes away by car, believe me, you will not think of it after entering. Its predecessor was the castle built by Scottish missionary doctor Mei Tenggen. Located on the top of Mogan Mountain at an altitude of 800 meters, it overlooks the panorama of Mogan Mountain.
The European-style castle on the top of the mountain is the landmark of naked Castle. When you check in, the front desk will give you a map. There are many online celebrity check-in points throughout the hotel, which is very fun.
Picture 1 was taken overlooking the hotel from Mogan Mountain.
Figure 2 is the hotel reception center. After arriving at the hotel, a car will come and pick up the guests to the reception center for check-in. After adding Mia, the lady at the front desk, to WeChat, you can use WeChat while you are in the hotel, and you can make arrangements at any time, which is very convenient. It is equivalent to one-on-one service of butler.
Figure 3 is the interior of the room. Many welcome snacks and drinks are free.
Figure 4 The exterior of the room. The winding path leads to a secluded place, and the scenery is very beautiful.

Figures seven and eight are all inside the castle. After turning on the lights at night, the path leading to the castle is romantic and beautiful. After dinner, you can enjoy the sunset at the castle.

msg:When people reach middle age, the pace of work accelerates, the children's academic growth, and the impact of the epidemic, the opportunity to travel becomes rare. Therefore, this summer, I decided to go for a light-luxury surrounding tour. Although there were some twists and turns at the start, as the car approached Moganshan, the instrument panel showed the falling outdoor temperature (10 degrees lower than Shanghai), and the mood became more cheerful. The castle built on the top of Mogan Mountain not only has a mysterious and exotic style, but also has a unique geographical location surrounded by green mountains and green waters. The chic cliff restaurant, the infinity heated swimming pool, the romantic European-style castle, the comfortable cliff-view suites, the sumptuous Chinese and Western delicacies, and the considerate butler service make "naked castle" the most popular resort in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. "Naked Heart" means to regain the passion and simplicity of the original heart, return to nature, enjoy family and friendship, and regain the balance of body and mind in simple happiness. Isn't that what travel is all about?

msg:If you are lucky enough to read this review, I suggest you choose another hotel. The service and facilities are not worthy of his price.
There are 4 families in our group, including two children. It took three years for the epidemic to finally make an appoin**ent. When everyone is free, we came to Moganshan once. We chose naked Castle after thousands of choices. Looking at the promotional photos of the hotel, Looking at the four-bedroom villa, I felt that it was a detached house with a very good view from the window, so I decided to make a reservation. When we arrived at the hotel, the hotel was very considerate and told us that we were upgraded to a five-bedroom villa because we were traveling with two children. We were very happy at the time and felt that the hotel was very humane. ignorance. This room type is called Mulan Courtyard. Friends who hope to see it stay carefully. After we got to the room, we were very disappointed. This room is on the same main road as another room. There is no yard in front of the door. There is a corridor leading to the back. There is no sun at all in the small courtyard. There are 5 rooms and 2 are outside, one of which cannot be exposed to the sun at all, and the other one can only be reached through the courtyard. At that time, there was no other way except disappoin**ent. Almost, I just felt that more than 10,000 yuan a night was not worth it. When I was about to wash up at night, I realized how poor the shower equipment in the room was. The water from the shower was as small as tears, there were hairs on the wall, the ceiling was cracked, and the living room was smelly. The stench, the sewer blockage and the smell, and the engineering depar**ent came several times, telling us that it must not be fixed tonight. At this time, we suggested to the hotel that we should change back to a 4-bedroom villa. This is the key point. , it turns out that the 4-bedroom villas in the hotel are oversold. There are no 4-bedroom villas anymore, and the hotel manager is no longer there. The manager on duty told us that it would be too much for one night to change to a 3-bedroom villa. Room 4 will only be available tomorrow. After negotiating all night, finally on the second day, we were given back to the original 4 room called Gaoshan Courtyard. We were surprised when we got to room 4. The view in front of the window was much better. The room facilities are also much better. Most of the whole trip was spent changing rooms, waiting for the room, and it was not until 3 pm the next day that we officially settled in the room we originally booked, and we had to check out at noon on the third day. Although the hotel has made up for the first day's room rate, the wasted time and the unpleasantness of the trip cannot be made up for by the hotel. Here is a reminder to friends who can read this article, not all hotel upgrades are well-intentioned.
Hygiene: very poor, there is hair in the bathroom, and the floor is dusty.
Environment: Depends on the room, Mulan Courtyard is a mess, don't stay here. The restaurant is also very old. In addition to taking pictures, you can tell how old it is at a glance.
Facilities: facilities are very old
Service: The waiters all feel like interns, and there is no manager on duty. If you have any questions, ask the waiter, saying that they have all gone to eat, but no one handles it. Simply speechless. Waiting for half an hour for the shuttle bus is commonplace. Those who can walk can walk by themselves. When returning to the room from the parking lot, you have to wait for the bus, which lasts for half an hour.

msg:Family stay. A group of 4 of us originally booked a two-bedroom courtyard for 8,000 per night for two nights. When we checked in, probably because of the epidemic, we only had another one to stay on that day, and we were upgraded to a 1w3/night three-bedroom courtyard. It was a surprise.
Because of the comfortable stay and the desire to visit the mountain scenery, we stayed for another night. We stayed here for four days and three nights in total. With a very leisurely and slow lifestyle, the vacation index was full.

Room facilities: The two-story building and the three rooms are similar in layout. The room area is not large, but the living room, kitchen and activity room on the first floor have a total interior area of more than 250 square meters, which is also very spacious and comfortable. In the yard, in addition to the long table, round table, chairs and barbecue, there is also a flowing outdoor hot spring pool unexpectedly, which must be soaked every night, awesome~
The details of the decoration style are very tasteful. I like the fireplace in the living room very much. The next day I played with it because of the sudden cooling, which was very pleasant.
The only thing I'm not satisfied with is that the toiletries provided in the room are relatively general. At this price, the supplies are too cheap.

Service: After experiencing the whole stay in the hotel, the service is probably the place that needs to be complained the most. When I checked in at the front desk, I felt that the waiter's response was stiff and dull, and the details were not in place. The quality of the room cleaning staff was ok, but the first day cleaning was a bit flawed (forgot to add tea bags). But overall, it is still responsive, barely within the acceptable range.

Breakfast: Breakfast is served at Naked Western Restaurant. Due to the epidemic, it is currently in a semi-self-service form (hot food order + cold food self-service). We also had dinner at this restaurant during our stay, the portion is not much, but the taste is very üâë. Then the waiter in the restaurant is not bad in comparison~

Location: The hotel is located on Baotou, one of the hills of Mogan Mountain. The scenery is amazing. We can see a bamboo sea from the Weisock courtyard where we live, and next to it is the path leading to Baibuling and Moganshan Scenic Area. Almost every day, I go to the mountains for a walk and visit the scenic spots. During the few days I stayed, it happened to be rainy and sunny, and the various scenery was still unfinished.

The overall experience is very good, and I will most likely stay here again in the future~
